The bathtub is designed between the room and the bathroom, so that the bathtub is usually used as a decoration. This time, I have the urge to use it once (this is the biggest discovery this time). The design is very practical. The two ends of the bathtub are very spacious and you can put all the food and other items you want to take a bath. The main thing is that it is open and not oppressive. The bathroom door also opens inwards, unlike other hotels that open outwards. The floor towel on the ground is basically a decoration. This is the characteristic of this resort hotel that is different from other hotels.

msg:During the Spring Festival, I brought my wife and parents to stay in two suites in Mei Shang.
After two days of experience, from the initial expectations to the rush to leave the store, I was slightly disappointed. The summary is that the new team has no experience. They know their mistakes but do not correct them. In order to make money, they care too much about the customers. The specific points are:

1. The traffic is a bit difficult. The hotel is in a scenic area, so you need to park your car and check in. You have to walk for 20 minutes, which is unbearable on rainy days.

2. The rooms are facing each other seriously. Please bring your own headgear when checking in. The hotel is in a swastika shape, with a circle of guest rooms outside and suites in the atrium. There is no privacy at all. You can clearly see people dressing and undressing on the opposite side (no offense intended). The bed was also deliberately facing the window, and the curtains were kept closed throughout the stay. In order to keep the occupancy rate, more than 2,000 yuan was sold to the guests. The guests who could afford it would get mad if they stayed.

3. I asked to change to a peripheral room, but refused because the room was full. Later, I learned that the occupancy rate that day was less than 70%, so I was really afraid of getting my money back.

4. The bathroom smells bad, and the bathroom is still open in the bedroom. There is a faint smell all night. The key is that my wife is pregnant.

5. The meal was probably just opened, so the reception capacity was not high. I waited for 40 minutes to be seated in the Chinese restaurant, but no food was served, so I went out to eat. Breakfast was closed too early. The front desk told us that it would be 11 o'clock. We came at 10 o'clock, but half of it had already been withdrawn. They said it would be moved to the front. I understand that you are controlling costs, but it was uncomfortable.

6. The scenic spots have beautiful scenes and a lot of inves**ent, but there are few businesses and complaints are concentrated in these areas. My family was spending money in a teahouse. I guess the paint on the furniture was not fully dry due to the rush to open. A few pairs of pants were stained by the paint and were considered useless, as were several guests in the teahouse. We did not embarrass the staff. After complaining on the spot, we called the customer service and asked for a quick exit.
But what was promised on the spot has not yet been resolved. When it comes to compensation, they emphasize that they are only willing to pay the cleaning fee. It is probably due to insufficient authorization and heavy KPIs. The staff generally admit their mistakes and do not correct them.

In short, as a new project, Puyuan has beautiful scenic scenes, but the accommodation hardware and pricing are slightly insufficient. However, the unfamiliarity in service offsets the room premium brought by the scenic spot. The team is inexperienced and has a good attitude but lacks authorization. So far, no depar**ent has come out to take responsibility for customer complaints.
For tourists, vacation is a comprehensive experience. Whether it is a hotel or a scenic spot, it is a whole. Each depar**ent has its own assessment. If the boundaries between depar**ents are too clear, it will affect the evaluation of the entire project.
I hope the management will strengthen their efforts and wish the project better and better.
